			lower_house_next_resolution_check = { resolution = resolution_galacticcooperation_repeal_1 }
			lower_house_next_resolution_check = { resolution = resolution_galacticcooperation_repeal_2 }
			lower_house_next_resolution_check = { resolution = resolution_galacticcooperation_repeal_3 }

			lower_house_next_resolution_check = { resolution = resolution_galacticcooperation_interstellar_mediation }
			lower_house_next_resolution_check = { resolution = resolution_galacticcooperation_sanctity_of_life }
			lower_house_next_resolution_check = { resolution = resolution_healthcare_repeal_1 }
			lower_house_next_resolution_check = { resolution = resolution_healthcare_repeal_2 }
			lower_house_next_resolution_check = { resolution = resolution_healthcare_repeal_3 }
			lower_house_next_resolution_check = { resolution = resolution_healthcare_repeal_4 }
			lower_house_next_resolution_check = { resolution = resolution_healthcare_repeal_5 }
			lower_house_next_resolution_check = { resolution = resolution_healthcare_board_of_health }
			lower_house_next_resolution_check = { resolution = resolution_healthcare_xenomedical_research }
			lower_house_next_resolution_check = { resolution = resolution_healthcare_war_relief }
			lower_house_next_resolution_check = { resolution = resolution_healthcare_clonal_medicine }
			lower_house_next_resolution_check = { resolution = resolution_healthcare_universal_healthcare }
			lower_house_next_resolution_check = { resolution = resolution_repeal_protect_neutrals }
			lower_house_next_resolution_check = { resolution = resolution_protect_neutrals }
		}
		# 开始会议
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { which = lh_next_resolution_score value > 0 } }
			set_lower_house_ongoing_flag = yes
			generate_weight_random_change = yes
			monthly_set_lh_voting_weight = yes
			# 开始局势
			every_galcom_member = {
				start_situation = {
					type = situation_galactic_lower_house
					target = event_target:lh_recent_proposer
				}
				create_message = {
					type = MESSAGE_LOWER_HOUSE_IN_SESSION
					localization = MESSAGE_LOWER_HOUSE_IN_SESSION_DESC
					days = 12
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							is_same_value = event_target:lh_recent_proposer
							AND = {
								is_ai = yes
								check_variable = { which = lhw_resolution_recent value >= 7 }
							}
						}
					}
					every_situation = {
						limit = { is_situation_type = situation_galactic_lower_house }
						set_situation_approach = lower_house_approach_support
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						is_ai = yes
						check_variable = { which = lhw_resolution_recent value <= 5.5 }
					}
					every_situation = {
						limit = { is_situation_type = situation_galactic_lower_house }
						set_situation_approach = lower_house_approach_oppose
					}
				}
				else = {
					every_situation = {
						limit = { is_situation_type = situation_galactic_lower_house }
						set_situation_approach = lower_house_approach_abstain
					}
				}
				# 调整时间表
				every_situation = {
					limit = { is_situation_type = situation_galactic_lower_house_schedule }
					export_trigger_value_to_variable = {
						trigger = situation_progress
						variable = situation_progress_var
					}
					multiply_variable = { which = situation_progress_var value = -1 }
					add_situation_progress = situation_progress_var
					add_situation_progress = 67
				}
			}
			# 设置初始选项
			every_galcom_member = { #非附庸
				limit = {
					OR = {
						is_subject = no
						overlord = { is_galactic_community_member = no }
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							is_same_value = event_target:lh_recent_proposer
							AND = {
								is_ai = yes
								check_variable = { which = lhw_resolution_recent value >= 7 }
							}
						}
					}
					every_situation = {
						limit = { is_situation_type = situation_galactic_lower_house }
						set_situation_approach = lower_house_approach_support
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						is_ai = yes
						check_variable = { which = lhw_resolution_recent value <= 5.5 }
					}
					every_situation = {
						limit = { is_situation_type = situation_galactic_lower_house }
						set_situation_approach = lower_house_approach_oppose
					}
				}
				else = {
					every_situation = {
						limit = { is_situation_type = situation_galactic_lower_house }
						set_situation_approach = lower_house_approach_abstain
					}
				}
			}
			every_galcom_member = { #附庸
				limit = {
					is_subject = yes
					overlord = { is_galactic_community_member = yes }
				}
				if = { #投票受限
					limit = {
						any_agreement = {
							OR = {
								has_term_value = { term = subject_diplomacy value = subject_can_not_do_diplomacy }
								has_term_value = { term = subject_diplomacy value = subject_can_do_diplomacy_but_not_vote }
							}
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							overlord = {
								any_situation = {
									is_situation_type = situation_galactic_lower_house
									current_situation_approach = lower_house_approach_support
								}
							}
						}
						every_situation = {
							limit = { is_situation_type = situation_galactic_lower_house }
							set_situation_approach = lower_house_approach_support
						}
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = {
							overlord = {
								any_situation = {
									is_situation_type = situation_galactic_lower_house
									current_situation_approach = lower_house_approach_oppose
								}
							}
						}
						every_situation = {
							limit = { is_situation_type = situation_galactic_lower_house }
							set_situation_approach = lower_house_approach_oppose
						}
					}
					else = {
						every_situation = {
							limit = { is_situation_type = situation_galactic_lower_house }
							set_situation_approach = lower_house_approach_abstain
						}
					}
				}
				else = { #自由投票
					if = {
						limit = {
							OR = {
								is_same_value = event_target:lh_recent_proposer
								AND = {
									is_ai = yes
									check_variable = { which = lhw_resolution_recent value >= 7 }
								}
							}
						}
						every_situation = {
							limit = { is_situation_type = situation_galactic_lower_house }
							set_situation_approach = lower_house_approach_support
						}
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = {
							is_ai = yes
							check_variable = { which = lhw_resolution_recent value <= 5.5 }
						}
						every_situation = {
							limit = { is_situation_type = situation_galactic_lower_house }
							set_situation_approach = lower_house_approach_oppose
						}
					}
					else = {
						every_situation = {
							limit = { is_situation_type = situation_galactic_lower_house }
							set_situation_approach = lower_house_approach_abstain
						}
					}
				}
			}
			# 调整时间表
			every_situation = {
				limit = { is_situation_type = situation_galactic_lower_house_schedule }
				export_trigger_value_to_variable = {
					trigger = situation_progress
					variable = situation_progress_var
				}
				multiply_variable = { which = situation_progress_var value = -1 }
				add_situation_progress = situation_progress_var
				add_situation_progress = 67
			}
			set_global_flag = lower_house_session_ongoing
			lower_house_voting_check = yes
			country_event = {
				id = MECR_LH.200
				days = 720
			}
		}
		else = { #无会可开，休会期延长一年
			remove_all_lh_next_resolution_flags = yes
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					any_situation = { is_situation_type = situation_galactic_lower_house_schedule }
				}
				every_situation = {
					limit = { is_situation_type = situation_galactic_lower_house_schedule }
					add_situation_progress = -16.5
				}
				if = {
					limit = { is_country_type = default }
					country_event = {
						id = MECR_LH.120
					}
				}
			}
			country_event = {
				id = MECR_LH.10
				days = 360
			}
		}
	}
}
country_event = { #120.无会可开，休会期延长一年通知
	id = MECR_LH.120
	title = "MECR_LH.120.title"
	desc = "MECR_LH.120.desc"
	is_triggered_only = yes
	picture = GFX_evt_arguing_senate

	option = {
		name = "MECR_LH.120.option"
	}
}
country_event = { #200.结束会议，根据投票结果通过或否决议案，定时下一次会议(10.)
	id = MECR_LH.200
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		is_same_value = event_target:global_event_country
		NOT = { has_global_flag = instant_stop_lh_session }
	}

country_event = { #1002.统计得票决定是否建立众议院(1010.1011.)
	id = MECR_LH.1002
	hide_window = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		set_variable = { which = lower_house_form_support value = 0 }
		set_variable = { which = lower_house_form_oppose value = 0 }
		# 统计得分
		every_galcom_member = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = lower_house_form_support }
			root = {
				change_variable = {
					which = lower_house_form_support
					value = prev.trigger:diplomacy_weight
				}
			}
			remove_country_flag = lower_house_form_support
		}
		every_galcom_member = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = lower_house_form_oppose }
			root = {
				change_variable = {
					which = lower_house_form_oppose
					value = prev.trigger:diplomacy_weight
				}
			}
		}
		# 通过，一个月后开始会议
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { which = lower_house_form_support value >= lower_house_form_oppose }
			}
			# 启用时间表局势
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { any_situation = { is_situation_type = situation_galactic_lower_house_schedule } }
				}
				start_situation = {
					type = situation_galactic_lower_house_schedule
					target = this
				}
			}
			every_situation = {
				limit = { is_situation_type = situation_galactic_lower_house_schedule }
				export_trigger_value_to_variable = {
					trigger = situation_progress
					variable = situation_progress_var
				}
				multiply_variable = { which = situation_progress_var value = -1 }
				add_situation_progress = situation_progress_var
				add_situation_progress = 64.25
			}
			every_galcom_member = {
				country_event = {
					id = MECR_LH.1010
				}
			}
			country_event = {
				id = MECR_LH.10
				days = 30
			}
			set_global_flag = lower_house_founded
			set_timed_global_flag = {
				flag = lower_house_form_succeed_timer
				years = 20
			}
			set_saved_date = {
				key = lower_house_form_succeed_date
				days_from_present = 7200
				expires = 7200
			}
			set_global_flag = form_galactic_lower_house_by_event
			pass_resolution_no_cooldown = resolution_form_galactic_lower_house
		}
		# 未获通过，仍能在参议院再次提出
		else = {
			set_global_flag = lower_house_form_failed
			set_timed_global_flag = {
				flag = lower_house_form_failed_timer
				years = 20
			}
			set_saved_date = {
				key = lower_house_form_failed_date
				days_from_present = 7200
				expires = 7200
			}
			every_galcom_member = {
				country_event = {
					id = MECR_LH.1011
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
